count ^NVnyCe68

let count = 10
function Counter() {
	function handleClick() {
		count++
		React.update()
	}
	return (
		<div>
			<span>Count: {count}</span>
			<button onClick={handleClick}>click</button>
		</div>
	)
}

function App() {
	return (
		<div id="app">
			<Counter />
		</div>
	)
}
